CHAPTER <span class="t0 t4 t5 t8 t12 t13 t15 t18 t23 t24 t26 t28 hoverable">VII</span>

WORSHIP*
Worship, puja, <span class="t22 t25 hoverable">individual</span> and collective,
plays a central part in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> of the Kaula.
There are different rituals for daily worship,
for the fortnightly and the monthly sessions.
Special rituals are prescribed for special occasions like the <span class="t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t14 t15 t17 t18 t19 t20 t24 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">days</span> of religious festivals, birthdays of one's own, of the Guru, the Parama
Guru etc. All are to be observed to the best of
one's ability, one's resources, the circumstances,
the times, the customs. In the selection,
assemblage and utilisation of the ingredients of
worship, the utmost care is to be exercised.
Much more than the material side of the
worship, the upasaka has to be careful of his
psychological <span class="t0 t1 t10 t14 t21 t23 t25 t29 hoverable">state</span> of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> and soul. Especially
in the <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> w i t h the Five M's, it is laid down
that they are to be <span class="t0 t12 hoverable">used</span> as prescribed purely for
the delectation of the Deity; if <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> creeps in
then it becomes a sinful act. T h e worshipper
shall bow down to the woman, who is to be
worshipped in certain rituals - m a r k that she
may be of any age from one year onwards for
purposes of <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> of the maiden, kumari
puja - as a deity, devata buddhya. The Deity is to
be first invoked in her and then the <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span>
proceeded with, w i t h a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> <span class="t1 t8 hoverable">free</span> from, impurity,
nirvikarena cetasa. At the best, the worshipper
himself must rise in his <span class="t0 t1 t13 t16 t24 t25 hoverable">consciousness</span> to the
status of a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">god</span> - devata-bhavam-asthitah.
* Ullasas 10, 11.

KULARNAVA TANTRA

The Yantra is an essential part of the Kaula
<span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> a proper Yantra the Deityis not pleased to be present. And where <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span>
is offered according to the scripture, the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Lord</span>
himself w i t h the Devi is present. Millions are
the attendants charged by Him with the protection of the Kula Dharma and of those who adhere
to it. T h e y are ever pleased when they are
remembered and given their due in worship.
Some of them, the major deities, are to be
invoked in the prescribed forms and worshipped.
Before entering the r i t u a l of <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> the
initiate shall cleanse himself w i t h purificatory
bath. He shall seat himself in the prescribed
manner and abstain from loose unconnected
talk. He shall not <span class="t6 hoverable">eat</span> before-hand. He shall
not lack in devotion and shall not be tainted
with greed in any form. He shall not offer
<span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> in the presence of one who is not
qualified to participate in the r i t u a l i.e. the
pasu, the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span> still in the a n i m a l stage as he is
not sufficiently purified in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> and soul.
It makes a big difference in the Kaula
<span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span> the worshipper is an enlightened <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> in the ways of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Knowledge</span> or
he is an ignorant man. T h e wise, says the
Tantra, intoxicated with the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> of the ritual,
do japa, meditate, praise, prostrate, instruct,
query, delight themselves during the sessions.
But the ignorant wander, roar, laugh, argue,
weep, <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> for sex and cavil. Slight, garrulousness, argumentation <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> logic, indifference, fear, anger, these are to be avoided in
the Circle of Puja. No quarter shall be given to
egotism. All are eligible to respect in the <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span>
of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span> Kaula. Nobody shall claim superio-

rity over others saying he is the Guru or he is

perform his <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> on suitable occasions.

any such
Pay respect to womankind, as they are all

Vishnu). Like the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">water</span> <span class="t0 t1 t4 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">within</span> the shell of a

common women open to the public gaze; but
not so the Sambhavi Vidya - the Science of the
Kaula - which is like the bride of a <span class="t17 t29 hoverable">high</span> family.
And the main-spring of this Kula Dharma lies
not in elaborate rituals like abhiseka, not in
Mantra, not in ponderous study of learned
treatises, but in a truthful ordering of life.
Proclaim the <span class="t3 t22 t28 hoverable">glory</span> of the Guru but guard the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">holy</span> Mantra imparted to you. The Guru is the
saviour. And more. Just as the sins of the

CHAPTER <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t21 t22 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">VIII</span>

DEVOTION TO GURU *
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> him, <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> his feet,

paduka. Just as the essence of Speech is there
below in the basic centre, muladhara, just as the
lowest in the rung - the sudras and the like - are
the effective instrumentations, similarly in the
Ocean of Kula all <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> is founded on the
paduka.
Remember and cherish this paduka
which yields infinitely more merit than any
<span class="t8 t21 t27 hoverable">number</span> of observances, gifts, sacrifices, pilgrimages, mantra-japa and rituals of worship. It is
that which, remembered, protects in times
of distress and danger and calamity. Study,
remembrance, knowledge, donations and sacrifices and <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> are truly done by him who
ever remembers on the tip of his tongue the
Mantra of this paduka. Look towards the direction in which the lotus feet of the Guru lie and
bow to it every <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">day</span> with devotion. There is no
mantra <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> than that of the paduka, no <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">god</span>
<span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> than the Guru, no initiation than that of
the Sakta and no merit <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> than the Kula
worship. At the root of dhyana is the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> of
the G u r u ; at the root of puja is the feet of the
Guru; at the root of the mantra is the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">word</span> of
the Guru and at the root of all liberation is the
grace of the Guru. are rooted in the G u r u ; <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">therefore</span> is the Guru to

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">holy</span> Guru. The beautiful mantra of the paduka
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> root is in the grace of the Guru, loaded

Hence shall the disciple do what is pleasing
to the Guru, by his mind, speech, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> and
action. When the Guru so pleased says, 'You

From his transcendent station, the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Lord</span> in the

Why the pains of <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> pilgrimages? Why

prostrate as prescribed.*

KULARNAVA TANTRA

Do not approach royalty, the Deity and the
Guru empty-handed. Offer in the measure of
your capacity, fruit, flower, cloth and the like.
Regard the Shakti of the Guru, the Guru's
son, his elder brother as the Guru himself. The
knower of the self shall look after the younger
brother of the Guru as his own son. Bow to the
Teacher of the Kula, to the eldest and the
youngest of the Guru, to one who is almost like a
Guru, as to your own Guru. Elder in the sacrifices, elder in order, elder in Kula, the eldest of
the Guru's sons, these are the four elders.
Respect them in that order, in the prescribed
manner.
To the elders like your father, mother and
other worthy relations, express your sentiment
by getting up, prostration and so on But should
you pose to be a teacher yourself, then these
acts become i l l of you.
Attained to the status of the Lord, pati, do
not bow down to any in the grade of the animal,
pasu He who attains to the status of the Guru
by meditation on the Mantra of the Padukat he
is to be esteemed as the Guru.

obtains no fruit whatever either here or there,
getting a Guru w h o knows not the T r u t h .
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Three</span> are the Gurus among the Shaivas; five
among the Vaishnavas; hundreds in the Vedas
and Sastras. But in the K.ula there is only one
Guru.
The Gurus are of six kinds *:
* Different traditions have different classifications of
the Gurus. There is for instance one tradition which
speaks of twelve kinds of Gurus:
1. Dhatuvadi Guru who ensures liberation by making
the disciple practice sadhana, observances and so on.
2. Candana Guru who emanates his <span class="t17 t29 hoverable">high</span> <span class="t0 t1 t13 t16 t24 t25 hoverable">consciousness</span> like the sandal tree giving out its fragrance and
imparting it to other trees in its environs. His mere
proximity acts for liberation.
3. Vicara Guru who acts on the <span class="t5 t15 t21 t27 hoverable">intelligence</span> of the
disciple and leads him through subtler and subtler operations of the buddhi.
4. Anugraha Guru who uplifts by sheer grace.

GURU-SHISHYA

99

Preraka, impeller, who impels interest that
leads to initiation; Sucaka, indicator, who
indicates the sadhana in which interest has been
awakened; Vacaka, explainer, who explains the
process and its object; Darsaka, shower, who
shows definitely the working and its aim in
greater detail; Siksaka, teacher, who actually
teaches how to do sadhana; Bodhaka, Illuminator, who lights up in the disciple the l a m p of
knowledge, mental and spiritual. Of these, the
first five are, as it were, the effects of the last as
the Cause. For it is only the understanding
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> imparted by the Bodhaka that brings
5. Parasa Guru whoso mere touch, like that of parasa
(philosopher's stone) transmutes the disciple.
6. Kacchapa Guru who redeems the disciple merely
by thinking of him, like the Kacchapa, tortoise, nourishing its young ones by <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> alone.
7. Candra Guru <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> natural rays melt the being
of the disciple in the manner of the chandrakanta stone
(moon-stone) oozing out at the rays of the moon.
8. Darpana Guru who like a mirror reveals the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span>
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> (of yourself and the universe) when you meet him.
9. Chayanidhi Guru, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> mere shadow confers
divinity on you even as the shadow of the bird Chayanidhi
is said to confer kinghood on whomsoever falls its
shadow.
10. Nadanidhi Guru who like the precious stone of
that name, which transmutes any metal into gold the
moment its sound reaches it, gives <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Knowledge</span> the moment
the <span class="t8 t13 t21 hoverable">call</span> of the aspirant reaches him.
11. Krauncapaksi
Guru <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> mere remembrance
confers <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> elevation on the disciple like the
remembrance by the Krauncapaksi feeding its young ones
in a far away place.
12. Suryakanta Guru, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> mere glance burns up the
sins of the disciple like the rays of the <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t7 t9 t10 t11 t12 t14 t15 t16 t18 t19 t21 t22 t24 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">sun</span> burning cotton
and the like when they fall on it through the sun-crystal.

to fruition all that is contributed by the rest.
Instigation, inauguration, explanation, direction
and teaching <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> remain barren unless they
are <span class="t2 t5 t11 t18 t19 t23 t26 hoverable">taken</span> up and assimilated in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Knowledge</span>
that is lit.
There may be m a n y Gurus. But only his
feet-sandals are to be worshipped who is competent to perform the Purna-abhiseka (ceremony
of <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span> bathing).
Having once obtained a Guru who is endowed
with features, who cuts asunder all doubt and
gives <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> excellently, do not resort to
another. But should you have a Guru w h o does
not have the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and always creates
doubt, no blemish attaches to you if you go to
another. Like the bee greedy for honey going
from flower to flower, the disciple eager for
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> goes from Guru to Guru.
We may observe here that this freedom to
go from Guru to Guru has its own advantages
and disadvantages. Each Guru has his own w a y
of approach and communication. T h e seeker is
the gainer for meeting many who are advanced
on the Path. His horizon widens, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> becomes
more catholic But he is disciple to nobody and
the responsibility to pool <span class="t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t22 t23 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">together</span> a l l that he
receives and organise it purposively for his selfadvancement lies squarely on his own shoulders.
On the other <span class="t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">hand</span> if one is fortunate to <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> the
right Guru he takes himself to him in fullness
and if the Guru accepts h i m as his disciple, then
according to all <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> tradition the Guru
takes charge of his <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> life. The responsibility rests with the Guru as <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> as that
relation is allowed to continue.

DIKSHA (INITIATION)*
It is laid down by the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Lord</span> that there can be
no moksa, liberation, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> diksa, initiation;
and initiation cannot be there <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> a Teacher,
hence it comes down the line of Teachers,
parampara.
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Without</span> a Teacher, all philosophy,
traditional knowledge, Mantras are fruitless.
Him alone the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">gods</span> laud who is the Guru
keeping active what is handed down by tradition, who is <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">well</span> versed in the Mantras and
Agamas and guards the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> of the Samaya
(Traditional) Doctrine. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Though</span> himself unattached, the Guru, after testing him for some
time, on command of the Lord, shall deliver
(the truth) to his disciple, in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> to vest him
with authority. Of h i m who is so invested
with authority, there is verily union with the
Supreme Shiva; at the termination of the bodily
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> his is the <span class="t0 t28 hoverable">eternal</span> liberation - this is declared
by the Lord. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> should one seek with
all effort to have a Guru of the unbroken Tradition <span class="t9 t24 hoverable">born</span> of the supreme Shiva himself.
After testing the disciple in the prescribed
manner for the fruition of the Shakti and for
happy success, the Guru shall communicate to
h i m the Mantra; otherwise it will be fruitless.
If one gives contrary to this requirement, if
one receives contrary to it, both he who gives
and he who receives shall stand cursed for generations. If, out of delusion, the Guru and the

disciple give and receive the instruction <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span>
prior mutual testing, they suffer condemnation.
So too if the instruction is contrary to the Scripture, both he who gives and he w h o receives
suffer perdition. He who imparts instruction

Initiating according to the
tradition, giving its paduka (Mantra), seating the

The <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> that is

Whatever know ledge is imparted
to the bad and undevoted disciple, it becomes

To initiate one who is unfit by <span class="t1 t11 t16 t20 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">reason</span> of

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and in action, shall the Guru test the
disciple with effort for the period of one year or
half or quarter <span class="t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t17 t18 t19 t20 t22 t23 t27 t29 hoverable">Bring</span> the <span class="t17 t29 hoverable">high</span> to the low, the
low to the high, in matters concerning life,
money, prostration, commands just and otherwise. He who does not grieve on <span class="t1 t11 t12 t13 t16 t18 t21 t23 t24 t26 t29 hoverable">account</span> of
such delusive cruel doings, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">words</span> corresponding
to these doings, frequent partialities, indifferences, several and repeated, <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span> pulled or
beaten, always takes it as the Grace of the Guru.
T h e y who thrill with joy, tremor, horripilation
and change in voice, <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> etc. at the remembrance of the Guru, in his laudation, in his

DIKSHA (INITIATION)

audience, in prostration to him, in his service,
in calling him and sending him off - they are fit
to be inducted in the purification for initiation.
T h e disciple also shall test the Guru in
similar signs of joy etc. in japa, stotra, dhyana,
homa, puja and so on. After knowing his capacity for transmission of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> perfection
in the science of Mantra, ability to make subtle
impact, one is to become his disciple, not otherwise.
There are those who are competent in the
beginning, those competent in the middle and
those competent in the end, due to the transmission of the Guru's Shakti; these disciples are
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> the lowest, the middling and the best
respectively.
Those in w h o m there is devotion at the outset, when they come for initiation but <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span>
enthusiasm cools down soon, are the adiyogya,
competent in the beginning.
Those who arrive when the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> for initiation is at <span class="t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">hand</span> and have neither special nor a n y
knowledge, but <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> past is done a w a y with
by their devotion, are the madhyayogya, competent in the middle.
Those who have no devotion at the outset,
who have devotion in the middle and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span>
devotion is fully grown at the end are the
antayogya, competent at the end and known as the
best jnanins.
Instruction, upadesa, is of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> k i n d s : that
of karma, of dharma, of jnana. Of these the
instruction or path of karma proceeds slowly
like the ant which takes <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> to reach the fruit
at the top of the tree, proceeding slowly and
slowly. The path of dharma is like the pace of

104

KULARNAVA TANTRA

the monkey which strains, jumping from branch
to branch, and reaches the fruit. The path of
jnana is like that of the bird which flies straight
and rests on the fruit quickly.
Initiation, diksa, is of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> k i n d s : initiation
by touch, spared, initiation by sight, drksanjna,
initiation by thought, manasa - all these <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span>
are done <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> ritual, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> exertion.
Initiation and instruction by touch is likened
to the slow nourishing of its young by the bird
with the w a r m t h of its wings.
Initiation and instruction by sight is like the
nourishing of its young by the fish through its
seeing alone.
Initiation and instruction by <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> (subtle
impingement) is like the nourishing of its young
by the tortoise by only thinking of t h e m .
The disciple receives the Grace according
to the impact of the Shakti, saktipata; where
there is no impact of sakti, there is no fulfilment.
Altogether, diksa, initiation, that gives
liberation is said to be of seven k i n d s : diksa
through r i t u a l ; through letter; through special
emanation (kala); through touch; through
speech; through s i g h t ; through thought.
Diksa is also classified as f o l l o w s : samaya,
when it authorises the disciple to help the Guru
manually in puja etc.; putrika when it enjoins
on him to perform the ritual indicated; sadhika,
when it initiates h i m in the inner sadhana;
vedhaka, when it impinges subtly; purna-acharya
when it vests on one the <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span> competence of a
teacher; nirvana, when it leads to laya through
sadhana.
Eightfold again is diksa through outer ritual

DIKSHA (INITIATION)

105

in which kunda fire-bowl, mandapa, enclosure,
kalasa jar etc., are used; prescribed means are
to be adopted for the purification of the body.
Diksa of letter, varna is threefold depending
on <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span> the letters are 42 or 50 or 62 Letters
shall be placed on the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> of the disciple and
withdrawn in reverse order, joining his <span class="t0 t1 t13 t16 t24 t25 hoverable">consciousness</span> to the supreme Self. After withdrawal, the letters are to be again laid on the
<span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> of the disciple in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> of <span class="t0 t1 t5 t7 t9 t11 t12 t13 t16 t17 t20 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">creation</span>
and as prescribed; so too shall be exercised the
Consciousness. The <span class="t0 t1 t10 t14 t21 t23 t25 t29 hoverable">state</span> of godhood <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span> of
delight is <span class="t9 t24 hoverable">born</span> in the child (of the Guru). This is
the varnamayi diksa which removes all bonds.
Kala diksa is also threefold* to be done as
prescribed. Beginning from the base of the feet
up to the knee, it is nivrtti kala; from the knee
to the navel it is pratistha; from navel to the
neck it is vidya; from the neck to the forehead
it is santi; from there to the <span class="t1 t4 t9 t16 hoverable">head</span> it is
santyatita.
This is the graded spread of kaladiksa.
Following the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> of withdrawal, the
knower of the sequence, joins from <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> to
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> up to the head. This is the kala diksa of
38 parts or 50. Knowing from the Guru, following the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> of <span class="t0 t1 t5 t7 t9 t11 t12 t13 t16 t17 t20 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">creation</span> and withdrawal in the
placement of the tattvas, one shall center and
impinge on the disciple. Then is <span class="t9 t24 hoverable">born</span> the <span class="t0 t1 t10 t14 t21 t23 t25 t29 hoverable">state</span>
of godhead and the meeting with the yogins and
viras (higher beings). This is the kala diksa
which destroys the bonds of the pashu.

Invoking <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Lord</span> Siva in the hand, doing japa
as prescribed, the Guru shall touch the <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span>
of the disciple; this is sparSa diksa, tactual
initiation.
Securing the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> in the T r u t h , shall the

expansions of the supreme T r u t h ; that is the
vag-diksa, verbal initiation.
Closing the <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> and meditating <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> the
supreme Truth, with a happy <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> shall the
Guru gaze <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">well</span> into the disciple; that is drgdiksa, ocular initiation.
When by the mere look or speech or touch
of the Guru, there is an instantaneous Knowledge, that is sambhavi diksa.
Of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">two</span> kinds is mano-diksa, mental initiation - intense and highly intense, tivra and
tivratara.
Knowing the sixfold Route, adhva,
one shall <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> of the disciple, the
bhuvana, tattva, kala} varna, pada and mantra from the knee, navel, heart, neck, palate to top
of the head.
The <span class="t5 t8 hoverable">wise</span> shall effect the vedha (subtle
impact) following the method received from
the Guru. In a moment will the disciple in
bonds get freed from them. This is intense,
tivra, initiation yielding liberation.
Merely by remembrance on the part of the
Guru, proficient in the vedha, the disciple has
his <span class="t2 t5 t8 t17 t18 t19 hoverable">sin</span> severed; this is the highly intense,
tivratara diksa. Released from external activity
he falls on the ground instantly; a godly <span class="t0 t1 t10 t14 t21 t23 t25 t29 hoverable">state</span>
arises in him and he comes to know everything.
Whatever is there at that moment of impact, he
experiences it himself, but on waking up he is
unable to <span class="t6 t9 t11 t19 t20 t22 hoverable">speak</span> of that happiness. Struck by

such impact, one verily is a Shiva, he has no
more birth This is the tivratara diksa that
releases from the bonds of birth, yields the
very <span class="t0 t1 t10 t14 t21 t23 t25 t29 hoverable">state</span> of Shiva.
Of one so struck six are the states described:
joy, tremor, new birth, reeling, sleep, swoon.
These six characteristics are seen at the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> of
the impact. Wherever be the <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> so struck,
he is liberated; there is no doubt of it.
Difficult to get is such a Guru who can
initiate <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">thus</span> by subtle impact; difficult also is
the disciple fit for i t ; it is only by happy
conjunction of merit that he is obtained But
this initiation shall not be given to anybody and
everybody; such is the Command.
Duly worshipping the circle of the Kula with
appropriate ingredients of Kula worship, the
Guru shall show it to the disciple. This is the
kauliki diksa, initiation of the Kaula.
Filling the mouth with the substance for
<span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> mixed with the five nectarous products
of the cow*, the Guru shall bathe the disciple
with i t ; this is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> the gandusa dkisa, mouthful initiation.
Diksa is again twofold depending on <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span>
it is external, bahya, or internal, antara; the
external is kriya diksa (ritualistic initiation) and
the other, internal, is the vedha diksa (subtle
impact).
Purification is twofold, inner and o u t e r ; the
inner is effected by appropriate ritual, the outer
by diksa. By diksa, the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">light</span> of liberation, even
the lowest <span class="t9 t24 hoverable">born</span> is freed. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Without</span> these <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">two</span> the
Kaulika is not liberated.

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Though</span> the ritual be the same, these dlksas

As the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">power</span> of poison is killed by Mantra

From this extensive bondage diksa alone
liberates, by pointing out the supreme station
and leads to the <span class="t21 hoverable">ancient</span> <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">divine</span> Abode.
Diksa, given according to the prescribed
mode, burns up in a moment all ill-omens and
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">great</span> sins in their millions.
That by which the pasus (animal men) have
their <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> opened and become Shivas, is the diksa
which liberates from the bonds of the paSus.
That which instantly generates <span class="t7 t13 t19 t20 t29 hoverable">faith</span> and
conviction is diksa; the rest are only pleasing to
the populace.
That diksa <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> which there is no fulfil
ment even with a hundred upasanas, should be

Mantra.
As iron struck by mercury becomes gold so
does the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> struck by diksa attain to Shivahood
With all karma burnt out by diksat all bonds
of Maya severed, attaining to the supreme end of
Jnana, seedless*, he becomes Shiva.
Gone is the shudrahood of a shudra the
brahmanhood of a brahmana; there obtains no
distinction of caste where there is the effect of

CHAPTER XI

PURASCHARANA*
Among the various lines of self-elevation
prescribed to the seekers of the Truth, the
Kularnava lauds the Japa as the pre-eminent and
invests it with the sanctity and efficacy of a
yajna, sacrifice, for attaining the fourfold <span class="t24 t25 hoverable">object</span>
of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> viz. dharma, Right, artha, Wealth, Kama,
<span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">Desire</span> and moksa, liberation. All other means
can be <span class="t1 t7 t12 t29 hoverable">left</span> out and only the means of mantra i.e.
japa of mantra resorted to which is sure to yield
success if carried out <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> blemish But if it
is allowed to be tarnished with fault then its
fruit is indeed inauspicious. Japa is the happy
giver of enjoyment, salvation, self-fulfilling
wish. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> practise the Yoga of Japa and
Dhyana. All blemishes due to transgressions of
rule, from the Jiva up to the Brahma, done knowingly or unknowingly, are wiped away by Japa.
Should you <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> fulfilment in this <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span>
ridden heavily with unhappiness, doing Japa of
the Mantra with the five-limbed upasana you
w i l l attain happiness. Daily puja at the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span>
prescribed hours - in the morning, noon and
evening - japa, tarpana (offering of libation),
homa and feeding the Brahmanas is this fivefold
upasana <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> purascarana.
If any of these
limbs are lacking, make up for it with appropriate increase of Japa as prescribed. For no
fulfilment is possible if there be want of l i m b ;
hence attempt to <span class="t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t22 t24 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">set</span> it right by Japa w i t h
devotion.

<span class="t1 t8 hoverable">Free</span> from foreign elements, the wicked, the

only brings poverty, disease and misery. He
shall have a seat made of cotton wool, cloth,
skin of lion, tiger or deer; it brings <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">good</span> fortune,
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and increase. And seating himself
in an asana - padma, swastika of vira etc. - he
shall perform japa and puja. Otherwise they
w i l l be fruitless.

shall be joined to japa and

As i m p u r i t y of the mental is
burnt away when it is blown upon, the sins of
the senses are burnt out by the control of prana.
Whatever action is done by one who is purified
by Pranayama, that fructifies, undoubtedly, even
if done effortlessly. He who does this practice
regularly in accordance with the direction in the
Agama, attains the <span class="t0 t1 t10 t14 t21 t23 t25 t29 hoverable">state</span> of godhood and acquires
perfection in Mantra, mantrasiddhi.
Seeing h i m

if any one foolishly does the Mantra-japa <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> taking the precaution of nyasa etc. he is
harassed by all obstructions like the infant deer
by the tigers.

* The Tantra enumerates as many as sixty of these

being cognisant of these defects there is no fulfilment however much he may practise.
There are ten processes for the eradication
of these defects of Mantra: giving birth, giving
life, striking making aware, ceremonial bath,
cleansing of i m p u r i t y , satisfying, libation,
lighting, covering in protection. As weapons
rubbed on the whetstone get sharpened, Mantras
subjected to these processes acquire bloom.
For one who does the mantra-japa the Sastra
lays down what is to be eaten, what is to be
offered, the vegetable, roots, fruit, barley etc.
If any one acquires merit in the w a y of the
Dharma, nourished in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> by <span class="t0 t14 t23 t24 hoverable">food</span> and drink
from another, then half the merit belongs to the
donor of the <span class="t0 t14 t23 t24 hoverable">food</span> and half to the doer. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> an intelligent <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> shall, with all effort,
reject another's <span class="t0 t14 t23 t24 hoverable">food</span> during the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> of the
performance and of ritual for desired ends.
T h e tongue is burnt by the <span class="t0 t14 t23 t24 hoverable">food</span> of a n o t h e r ;
<span class="t20 hoverable">hands</span> burnt by accepting from a n o t h e r ; the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> burnt by (thoughts of) women of o t h e r s ;
how then can there be success in the endeavour?
If the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> be in one place, Shiva (passive consciousness) in another, Shakti (active consciousness) in another, and life-breath in still another
place, even a crore of japa is useless. All should
be gathered in one effort If learning is acquired
for the sake of debate, japa is done for the sake of
another, gifts given for the sake of fame, how can
there be fulfilment? If pilgrimage is done for the
sake of wealth, austerities for show, <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> of
deity for selfish purpose, how indeed can there
be fulfilment? Fools are they who do nyasa,
puja, japa, homa, w i t h a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> that is u n c l e a n ;
they all are fruitless. If the ritual is done by

117

one unclean due to faces, urine and other
leavings, then all japa, <span class="t0 t5 t11 hoverable">worship</span> etc. is rendered
i m p u r e . Him who makes japa with soiled cloth,
soiled hair, bad odour of mouth on his person,
the Deity being disgusted burns up in a moment.
Avoid during japa all laziness, yawning, sleep,
sneeze, spitting, fear, touching of lower limbs,
anger The mantra does not succeed where there
is excessive food, meaningless talk, gossip,
rigidity of rule, attachment to another, fickleness. Do not perform japa with a turban on,
w i t h cloak, naked, hair dishevelled, surrounded
by retinue, unclean upper cloth, or while i m p u r e
or while walking Avoid during Japa inertia,
grief, useless activity, <span class="t1 t8 hoverable">free</span> imagination and
passing of wind. Be calm, be clean, limited in
food, sleeping on ground, devoted, in <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span>
control, <span class="t1 t8 hoverable">free</span> from duality, steady of mind,
silent, self-controlled and do Japa. With
confidence, belief, composure, faith, regularity,
certitude, contentment, enthusiasm, and like
qualities, do Japa.
Success in japa lies in his <span class="t20 hoverable">hands</span> who is
decked with fragrant flowers, ornaments and
clothes. Devoted to the Mantra, with <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span>
dedicated to it, with <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> centred <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> it,
w h o l l y given to it, following its <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t17 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">meaning</span> and
meditating <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> it, do Japa of the Mantra.
When tired by japa, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">take</span> to dhyana; tired in
dhyana <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">take</span> again to japa. Of him who does
both japa and dhyana, the Mantra achieves anon.

APPENDIX A

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">WORD</span> - EXPLANATIONS
The seventeenth and the last Ullasa of the
Kularnava gives interesting derivations of many
of the important t e r m s in the Tantra Sastra
throwing a flood of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">light</span> on the height of aim
and the exactitude in detail of the wide-visioned
builders of this system. It begins with the Gurumantra, the prayer to the Guru:
" B o w to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thee</span> Oh Lord, to Shiva in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span>
of the Guru, who takest on many forms for the
purpose of the manifestation and the fulfilment
of the supreme Knowledge; who <span class="t1 t3 t4 t7 t8 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">art</span> in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span>
of Narayana, who <span class="t1 t3 t4 t7 t8 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">art</span> in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> of the supreme
Self, who <span class="t1 t3 t4 t7 t8 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">art</span> the <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t7 t9 t10 t11 t12 t14 t15 t16 t18 t19 t21 t22 t24 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">sun</span> dispelling the darkness of
all Ignorance, who <span class="t1 t3 t4 t7 t8 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">art</span> charged with cit, who
knowest all, who a r t the embodiment of compassion, who <span class="t1 t3 t4 t7 t8 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">art</span> the Auspicious. who givest
w h a t is auspicious to all devotees here and
beyond.
I bow to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thee</span> in front, at the sides, at
the back, above and below. As Sat-Chit, ordain
that I m a y ever be T h y servitor.
Guru: gu signifies darkness; ru what restrains it. He who restrains darkness (of ignorance) is the guru.
ga signifies giver of fulfilment; r, severer of
s i n ; u, Vishnu. He who contains all the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> in
himself is the supreme guru.
ga signifies wealth of knowledge; r, illumin a t o r ; u, identity with Shiva- He who contains
these in himself is the guru.

w h o are blind to the T r u t h of the Self and of the

Desika:
Because he wears the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> of the

Svami:
Because he exudes his inner,

Because he is devoid of the

Because he imparts the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span>

Space and Time, desakala, because he has

Samyami: Because he rejects misery due to

c o m p l e t e f r u i t , it is c a l l e d puja.
Arcana: B e c a u s e i t
yields the
desired
fruit,
abhistaphala,
h o l d s the fruit of a l l the
f o u r classes, caturvarga,
a n d d e l i g h t s , randanat,
a l l t h e gods, it is c a l l e d arcana.
Tarpana:
B e c a u s e t o t h e <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">God</span> t h a t i s t h e
Truth,
tattva,
s u r r o u n d e d b y His r e t i n u e ,
parivara,
it g i v e s n i n e f o l d d e l i g h t , navananda,
it is c a l l e d tarpana.
Gandha:
B e c a u s e it d e s t r o y s t h e affliction
of m i s f o r t u n e , d e e p a n d b o u n d l e s s , gambhira,
b e c a u s e it g i v e s k n o w l e d g e of dharma, it is
c a l l e d gandha.
Amoda:
B e c a u s e it c a u s e s t h e b i r t h of a l l
t h a t is b a s e d on S m e l l a g h r a n a n a (i.e. tattva, of
prithivi),
shows
the

of

moksamarga,
s u b j u g a t e s a l l c u r s e d g r i e f etc.,
daghdaduhkha, it is c a l l e d amoda.
Aksata:
B e c a u s e t h e y y i e l d food,
anna,
e l i m i n a t e c o m p l e t e l y , ksapita, a l l s i n , a n d m a k e
o n e identified w i t h T h a t ( t r u t h ) Tat, t h e y a r e
c a l l e d aksata.
Puspa:
B e c a u s e it i n c r e a s e s m e r i t , punya,
r e m o v e s the heap of sin, papa, y i e l d m u c h
wealth,
puskalartha,
it is c a l l e d puspa.
Dhupa:
Because it drives out c o m p l e t e l y ,

KULARNAVA TANTRA

Upasti:
S e r v i c e a t close q u a r t e r s a s p r e s cribed, by action, by mind, by speech, in all
s t a t e s is c a l l e d upasti.
Purascarana:
B e c a u s e it is d e a r to t h e
chosen Deity
by <span class="t1 t11 t16 t20 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">reason</span> of its five-limbed
a d o r a t i o n , it l e a d s in f r o n t of t h e d e v o t e e , purah
caratit it is c a l l e d purascarana
Arghya:
B e c a u s e it d e s t r o y s a l l s i n , aghat
because it increases wealth and
progeney,
b e c a u s e i t y i e l d s p r i c e l e s s f r u i t , anargha-phala,
it is c a l l e d arghya.
A n d finally, t h e ksetra, t h e s a c r e d Centre of
devotions is not a n y one particular <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> but
A l l t h i s t h a t i s m o b i l e a n d i m m o b i l e , etatcaracaram
sarvam; He w h o g u a r d s , p r o t e c t s
t h i s A l l i s t h e ksetrapala, t h e s u p r e m e G u a r d .
